 Richie Benno, known as the world's most famous voice of cricket, died in Sydney
 vah australian cricket ke lijend the
 He was 84 years old and had been battling cancer for a long time
 iske alaava saal 2013 main ghar ke paas hi hue ek car accident main ghayal hone ke baad se unki sehat thik nahin rahaa karti thi
 Beno was a strong Australian all-rounder
 saal 1964 main vah jab ritair hue, tab leg spinner ke taur par unke 248 wicket the
 He was the first cricketer to show more than 2000 runs in Test cricket and a double feat of over 200 wickets
 australia kii ore se unhone 63 test khele or inamen se 28 main captaini kii
 Beno proved to be the captain with no Test series lost under his captaincy
 haalanki iske baad unhone cricket kii duniya main sabase bade camentator or broadcaster ke taur par ubhare
 He was instrumental in improving the cricketing broadcast of the BBC and then the Australian channel Nine
 unki pahchaan duniya bhar main sabase pratishthit cricket awaz ke taur par hoti thi
 He also had a role in starting the 1997 Carrie Packer Series
 pichley do saal ko agar chhod den, to beno or australian cricket sijan ek-duusare ke poorak the

 The latest performance by Indian classical and contemporary dancer Akash Odedra is: Echoes (echoes)
 birmigham main janme or licester main rah rahe bhartiya mul ke 31 varshiya akaash antarrashtriya falak par samakaleen nrity ke teji se ubharate sitare hai
 In this latest performance, they stand on the stage , swinging the ghungroos like dancers, then presenting kathak among the ghungroo girls scattered around on the floor
 nrity main is pariklpana par, khaskar bharat kii shastreey nrity birdari main ho-hallaa much saktaa he
 After all, the Ghungroos are considered to be so sacred that the dancers worship them before every practice and presentation
 paramparawaadiyon ke liye yah uski pavitrataa kaa anadar he
 Aditi Mangaldas, choreographer and Kathak dancer of this dance performance, has similar feelings towards her ghungroos
 lekin ve darshakon se vaah-vaah karwaanaa or ugr pratikriyaaon se nibatna bhi jaanati hai
 Her dance performances have won the hearts of many and she also holds many foreign accolades
 vaise unke kuch aalochak bhi hai jo bharat tak simit hai or unki prastutiyon ko parampara se bhatka hua maanate hai
 Mangaldas has a rebellious attitude, due to which he rejected the Sangeet Natak Akademi Award in 2012 for his 'creative / contemporary' character
 ise ve tabhi sweekaar karatin jab use kathak ke liye diya jaataa
 Aditi knows how crazy the 'echoes' can be, but for them, ghungroos mean more than what she loves in the depths of her heart
 ahmedabad main 5 saal kii umr se kathak shuru karne vaaleen 55 varshiya mangaladas kahati hai, ''ghunghru mere har pal ke saathi rahe hai
 No matter how deeply you are attached to them, you have to leave, just as you have to leave your superstitions
 ghunghru aapaki lay or aapaki jindagi kii gunj hote hai
 "she further states that the 'echoes' have symbols for the molecules of DNA that initially surround the dancer and eventually take her into the lap
" 35 minute kii is nrity prastuti ke khatm hone par ghunghru odedra ke pairon main bandhe hote hai
 Mangaldas and Odedra, sitting on a diwan in their luxurious home in Delhi's military farms, have so many common characteristics that the two have had no problem working together
 donon ne hi prakhyat kathak koreographer or guru kumudini lakhiya se nrity siikhaa he
 Mangaldas later came to Delhi to learn from another great guru, Pandit Birju Maharaj

 layaaddh kalakaari, saaf-suthri daihik rekhaon or nirmitiyon par jor detaa he or mangaladas ne dhire-dhire apni prastuti ke maanakon ko itnaa ooncha uthaa diya ki apni nafis prakaash abhiklpana or manchasthal ke nipun istemaal se apni samooh koreography kaa unhone loha manavaa liya

 ve kahati hai, ''yah dekhnaa bahut chunauteepurn or dilachasp tha ki kya ho saktaa he or yah kitni dur tak ja saktaa he

 apni saat saal kii jaan-pahchaan main mangaladas odedra kii 'bhaavnaatmak aklmandi' se bhi prabhavit thim

 According to police, the woman was troubled by her married life and trapped in the superstition of black magic of the tantrik
 police ko ghatana kii jaankaree aaramail hospital prabandhan ne di, jahaan ilaaj ke dauraan peedit kii maut hui
 Police have identified the accused woman as KV Rama and Tantrik as Shyam Singh alias Bhagat
